effecti ve  f or  t he  m o bilizati o n  of  p eri p her al  bl o o d  ste m  cells  f or  a ut ol o g o us  tra ns pla ntati o n

re peat e x p os ures t o G- C S F a n d re p eat a p h eresis atte m pts.

a p pr o priate m o bilizati o n strate g y f or s u bjects wit h β -t halasse mia (Ya n n a ki et al., 2 0 1 3; Y a n na ki  et
